			var setREVStartSize=function(){
				try{var e=new Object,i=jQuery(window).width(),t=9999,r=0,n=0,l=0,f=0,s=0,h=0;
					e.c = jQuery('#rev_slider_10_1');
					e.gridwidth = [960];
					e.gridheight = [585];
							
					e.sliderLayout = "auto";
					if(e.responsiveLevels&&(jQuery.each(e.responsiveLevels,function(e,f){f>i&&(t=r=f,l=e),i>f&&f>r&&(r=f,n=e)}),t>r&&(l=n)),f=e.gridheight[l]||e.gridheight[0]||e.gridheight,s=e.gridwidth[l]||e.gridwidth[0]||e.gridwidth,h=i/s,h=h>1?1:h,f=Math.round(h*f),"fullscreen"==e.sliderLayout){var u=(e.c.width(),jQuery(window).height());if(void 0!=e.fullScreenOffsetContainer){var c=e.fullScreenOffsetContainer.split(",");if (c) jQuery.each(c,function(e,i){u=jQuery(i).length>0?u-jQuery(i).outerHeight(!0):u}),e.fullScreenOffset.split("%").length>1&&void 0!=e.fullScreenOffset&&e.fullScreenOffset.length>0?u-=jQuery(window).height()*parseInt(e.fullScreenOffset,0)/100:void 0!=e.fullScreenOffset&&e.fullScreenOffset.length>0&&(u-=parseInt(e.fullScreenOffset,0))}f=u}else void 0!=e.minHeight&&f<e.minHeight&&(f=e.minHeight);e.c.closest(".rev_slider_wrapper").css({height:f})
					
				}catch(d){console.log("Failure at Presize of Slider:"+d)}

			function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
					var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
					errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
					errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
					errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
					errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
						jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
				}

				<div id="post-10508" class="post-10508 page type-page status-publish hentry language-en">
			<span class="entry-title" style="display: none;">QWINCE One Page</span><span class="vcard" style="display: none;"><span class="fn"><a href="http://www.qwince.com/author/abuono/" title="Posts by Agostino Buono" rel="author">Agostino Buono</a></span></span><span class="updated" style="display:none;">2016-01-20T10:33:50+00:00</span>						<div class="post-content">
				<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box" style="padding-bottom: 0px; padding-top: 30px;">
<div class="fusion-row">
<h3 style="text-align: center; font-size: 28px; line-height: 60px; font-weight: 600;">Need help getting your ideas off the ground? That&#8217;s where we come in<br />
<a class="btn-default button medium button custom fusion-button button-flat button-pill button-medium button-lightgray button-8 buttonshadow-no" title="" href="http://youtu.be/t8FXSGl1NNI" target="_self" rel="prettyPhoto" type="button"><span class="fusion-button-text">Play Video</span></a></h3>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 80px; margin-top: 40px;"><img style="width: auto; max-width: 100%;" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/divider.png" alt="Digital Transformation" width="1280" height="31" /></div>
<div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box">
<div class="fusion-row ideas-row">
<div class="fusion-one-third one_third fusion-layout-column">
<div class="fusion-title title">
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="color: #e10707;">Five steps to make your ideas real</h2>
</div>
<p>Digital Transformation and Visionary Innovation know no bounds.<br />
With Qwince as your technology partner, your seed of an idea can grow, evolve and become reality.</p>
<ul class="fusion-checklist ideas-list">
<li class="fusion-li-item size-small"><span class="circle">I</span> <span class="fusion-li-item-content">Invent: we pinpoint opportunities</span></li>
<li class="fusion-li-item size-small"><span class="circle">D</span> <span class="fusion-li-item-content">Design: we engineer visionary innovation</span></li>
<li class="fusion-li-item size-small"><span class="circle">E</span> <span class="fusion-li-item-content">Execute: we build digital transformation</span></li>
<li class="fusion-li-item size-small"><span class="circle">A</span> <span class="fusion-li-item-content">Accelerate: we integrate wearables</span></li>
<li class="fusion-li-item size-small"><span class="circle">S</span> <span class="fusion-li-item-content">Secure: we secure internet of things</span></li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="fusion-two-third two_third fusion-layout-column last">
<div class="fusion-tabs fusion-tabs-1 classic vertical-tabs"><style type="text/css">.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li a{border-top-color:#ebeaea;background-color:#ebeaea;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs{background-color:#ffffff;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a:hover,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a:focus{border-right-color:#ffffff;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a:hover,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li.active a:focus{background-color:#ffffff;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs li a:hover{background-color:#ffffff;border-top-color:#ffffff;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .tab-pane{background-color:#ffffff;}.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .nav-tabs,.fusion-tabs.fusion-tabs-1 .tab-content .tab-pane{border-color:#ebeaea;}</style><div class="nav"><ul class="nav-tabs"><li class="active"><a class="tab-link" id="fusion-tab-invent" href="#tab-ef5b405cc3133a4887d" data-toggle="tab"><h4 class="fusion-tab-heading">Invent</h4></a></li><li><a class="tab-link" id="fusion-tab-design" href="#tab-27b01b440fd5e309bd1" data-toggle="tab"><h4 class="fusion-tab-heading">Design</h4></a></li><li><a class="tab-link" id="fusion-tab-execute" href="#tab-b775d41e47d95f02697" data-toggle="tab"><h4 class="fusion-tab-heading">Execute</h4></a></li><li><a class="tab-link" id="fusion-tab-accelerate" href="#tab-abc5c82f6409c6ef786" data-toggle="tab"><h4 class="fusion-tab-heading">Accelerate</h4></a></li><li><a class="tab-link" id="fusion-tab-secure" href="#tab-ae041eaa0b2c583a126" data-toggle="tab"><h4 class="fusion-tab-heading">Secure</h4></a></li></ul></div><div class="tab-content"><div class="tab-pane fade in active" id="tab-ef5b405cc3133a4887d"><br />
<i class="fa fontawesome-icon fa-lightbulb-o size-large large circle-yes" style="border-color: #f10123; background-color: #f10123; color: #ffffff;"></i></p>
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="font-size: 18px; color: #f10123;">INVENT: We are your digital innovation and digital transformation partner</h2>
<p style="text-align: left;">We’ll help you identify and utilise opportunities and challenges. <span style="color: #747474;">To do this, we conduct different research and digital transformation projects to find new products for our customer</span>.<br />
For example, we worked with <a title="Brunel University" href="http://www.brunel.ac.uk/" target="_blank">Brunel University</a> in London on <a title="MYO armband" href="http://www.getmyo.com" target="_blank">Thalmic Labs’ MYO</a> gesture control armband, to help elderly, disabled and low-mobility users to wirelessly control their favourite technologies.<img class="alignright wp-image-13846" style="margin: 10px;" title="Thalmic Myo" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/myo-armband-300x267.png" alt="Thalmic Myo" width="150" height="133" /></p>
<p style="text-align: left;">MYO is an emerging technology that lets us implement a new form of user interface that uses EMG signals from the forearm.<br />
Gestures are recognised before movement thanks to muscle activity and 9-axis inertial measurement unit (MEMS) MYO embeds a Bluetooth 4.0 Low Energy chip for connectivity.<br />
We are considering applications in the military, consumer and professional field.</p>
<p><a title="Electromechanics Research Program" href="http://qwince.com/portfolio-items/thalmic-myo-development-program/">Found out more in the &#8216;Our Work&#8217; section.</a></p>
<p></div><div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab-27b01b440fd5e309bd1"><br />
<i class="fa fontawesome-icon fa-pencil size-large large circle-yes" style="border-color: #f10123; background-color: #f10123; color: #ffffff;"></i></p>
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="font-size: 18px; color: #f10123;">DESIGN: We engineer visionary innovation</h2>
<p>Have a bright idea but don’t know what to do with it?<br />
<span style="color: #747474;">We are a group of highly skilled and experienced data scientist and engineers with plenty of technical expertise and passion…  </span></p>
<p><span style="color: #747474;">Digital Transformation in healthcare (m-Health and e-Health) is reality.</span> We are designing and developing a customisable digital framework for patient engagement and medication adherence solutions, which:<img class="alignright wp-image-13853" style="margin: 20px;" title="Empatica E4" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/e4-front_light-292x300.png" alt="Empatica E4" width="150" height="154" /></p>
<ul>
<li>combines education, reward, monitoring and screening to motivate the patients,</li>
<li>uses digital health devices (such as <a title="Empatica E4" href="https://www.empatica.com/e4-wristband" target="_blank">Empatica E4</a>, <a title="Cardiocity" href="http://www.cardiocity.com" target="_blank">Cardiocity</a>&#8230;) to collect reliable big data and improve the outcomes of therapy effectiveness,</li>
<li>sustain healthy behaviours thanks to gamifications and rewards,</li>
<li>involves different healthcare delivery organisations (HDO) and participants in the process,</li>
<li>provides advanced analytics to care providers based on big data.</li>
</ul>
<p><a title="Alchimya &amp; Cardiocity RhythmPad" href="http://qwince.com/portfolio-items/alchimya-cardiocity-rhythmpad/">Find out more in the &#8216;Our Work&#8217; section.</a><br />
</div><div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab-b775d41e47d95f02697"><br />
<i class="fa fontawesome-icon fa-cogs size-large large circle-yes" style="border-color: #f10123; background-color: #f10123; color: #ffffff;"></i></p>
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="font-size: 18px; color: #f10123;">EXECUTE: We build digital transformation</h2>
<p>With our background as a security integrator, our main priority is the security of your data and communications.  For example, we are designing and developing a secure identification system based on <a title="Nymi" href="http://www.getnymi.com" target="_blank">NYMI</a> technology.<img class="alignright wp-image-13850" title="NYMI" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/nymi-hero-300x300.png" alt="NYMI" width="200" height="200" /></p>
<p>NYMI has enormous potential to improve our lives, it works by using your unique electrocardiogram (ECG) signals to act as a biometric authentication layer for other devices, applications and services. So NYMI uses your heartbeat like a password to confirm your identity.</p>
<p>This system offers three authentication levels: the wristband itself, user&#8217;s unique cardiac rhythm and its mobile device, like a smartphone or tablet.</p>
<p>Our mission is to enable the Digital Transformation.<br />
</div><div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab-abc5c82f6409c6ef786"><br />
<i class="fa fontawesome-icon fa-magic size-large large circle-yes" style="border-color: #f10123; background-color: #f10123; color: #ffffff;"></i></p>
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="font-size: 18px; color: #f10123;">ACCELERATE: We evolve wearable technology</h2>
<p>We build digital transformation culture, boost innovation capability and confidence in technology and data security.<br />
Wearable technology can introduce great changes in our future. Neuralya (our brand new product) is our acceleration and evolution project.<img class="alignright wp-image-13852" style="margin: 10px;" title="Emotiv EPOC+" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/section1-epoc-300x168.png" alt="Emotiv EPOC+" width="201" height="112" /></p>
<p>Based on a human behavior and biometric data collection platform by <a title="iMotions" href="http://imotionsglobal.com/" target="_blank">iMotion</a>, Neuralya looks at a set of physiological parameters (facial coding, eye tracking, skin conductance, EEG&#8230;), using wearable devices (such as <a title="Empatica" href="https://www.empatica.com/e4-wristband" target="_blank">Empatica E4</a>, Gazepoint Eye Tracking, <a title="Emotiv" href="http://emotiv.com/" target="_blank">Emotiv Epoc +.</a>..), to evaluate the rational, emotional and instinctual components behind your customers&#8217; choices.</p>
<p>Learn how to push the &#8220;BUY button&#8221; inside your customer&#8217;s brain. Click here.<br />
</div><div class="tab-pane fade" id="tab-ae041eaa0b2c583a126"><br />
<i class="fa fontawesome-icon fa-shield size-large large circle-yes" style="border-color: #f10123; background-color: #f10123; color: #ffffff;"></i></p>
<h2 class="title-heading-left" style="font-size: 18px; color: #f10123;">SECURE: We secure your Internet of Things</h2>
<p>Our platform and our skills help organisations to protect and manage their logical, physical and cloud-based data assets.</p>
<p>An example is HYLA EYES on VUZIX M100 smartglasses.<img class="alignright wp-image-13856" title="VUZIX M100" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/vuzix-smart-glasses_1-300x200.jpg" alt="VUZIX M100" width="200" height="133" /><br />
We are qualified as an early adopter by the VUZIX DEVELOPMENT PROGRAM. We prototyped our product Hyla Eyes on Vuzix M100.<br />
Hyla Eyes is a secure data collection and certification system based on mobile devices, allowing completely secure communication with a control room and rendering data collected in the field uneditable.</p>
<p>Digital tools are provoking significant changes in the way we work, communicate, and sell. This implies new opportunities and challenges, and has triggered the Digital Transformation of enterprises.</p>
<p><a title="Hyla Eyes on Vuzix M100" href="http://qwince.com/portfolio-items/hyla-eyes-vuzix-m100/">Find out more in the &#8216;Our Work&#8217; section.</a><br />
</div></div></div>
</div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 80px; margin-top: 80px;"><img style="width: auto; max-width: 100%;" src="http://qwince.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/divider.png" alt="Digital Transformation" width="1280" height="31" /></div>

<h4 style="text-align: center; color: #666; margin-top: 10px; margin-bottom: 80px; font-size: 22px;">We are extremely flexible and accessible, with offices in the UK and Italy</h4>
